# Test Suite

This document lists all test cases in the FitVibe backend and frontend codebases.

**Last Updated:** 2025-12-13

## Summary

### Backend Tests

- **Total Test Files:** 82
- **Total Test Cases:** 1245 (tests that run, excluding skipped/pending)
- **Total Test Cases (including skipped):** 1311
- **Test Files Location:** `tests/backend/`

### Frontend Tests

- **Total Test Files:** 87 (excluding visual and e2e tests)
- **Total Test Cases:** 965 (tests that run)
- **Test Files Location:** `tests/frontend/` (excluding `visual/` and `e2e/` subdirectories)

### Overall

- **Total Test Files:** 169 (82 backend + 87 frontend)
- **Total Test Cases:** 2210 (1245 backend + 965 frontend)

## Test Organization

The backend tests are organized into the following categories:

- **Unit Tests:** Module-level tests for services, repositories, controllers, and utilities
- **Integration Tests:** Cross-module flow tests (auth-session, feed-sharing, session-points, etc.)
- **Middleware Tests:** Authentication, authorization, rate limiting, CSRF, error handling
- **Repository Tests:** Data access layer tests
- **Service Tests:** Business logic tests
- **Controller Tests:** API endpoint tests
- **Contract Tests:** OpenAPI contract validation
- **Infrastructure Tests:** Database migrations, seeds, scripts

The frontend tests include:

- **Component Tests:** UI component tests
- **Page Tests:** Page-level integration tests
- **Hook Tests:** Custom React hooks tests
- **Service Tests:** API client tests
- **Accessibility Tests:** WCAG compliance tests
- **SSR Tests:** Server-side rendering tests
- **Store Tests:** Zustand store tests
- **Utility Tests:** Helper function tests

Note: E2E tests (Playwright) and visual regression tests are excluded from the unit test count as they are run separately.
